 Inventory.PickupMessage "Picked up a Soulsphere +100 HP"

  {
  Spawn:
    MEGA ABCD 4 BRIGHT
    Loop
  pickup:   
    TNT1 A 0 A_Jumpifinventory("Fiendtoken",1,"Funky")
    TNT1 A 0 A_Jumpifinventory("Kunaitoken",1,"Kunai") 
    TNT1 A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("Megasphere1")
    Stop
  Funky:

    TNT1 A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("Megasphere1")
    Stop
  Kunai:

    Stop
    }
}

  Height 18
  scale 0.025
  +INVENTORY.INVBAR
    +DONTGIB
  Inventory.MaxAmount 3
  Inventory.InterHubAmount 3
  Inventory.Icon "GASTSMN"
  Tag "Gaster Blaster Summon"
  Inventory.PickupSound "Gaster/pain"
  Inventory.Usesound"Gaster/Teleport"
  Inventory.PickupMessage "You picked up a Gaster Blaster Summon! (Use with extreme caution!)"

  Spawn:
    GSMN A -1 Bright
    Stop
  Use:
    GSMN A 0 A_SpawnItemEx ("Gastbox1", 48, 0, 1, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION, 1)
    Stop
  }
}

Actor mediportalbeam
{
  Radius 4
  Height 18
  +Noclip
  Yscale 4.0
  xscale 0.1
  RenderStyle ADD
  +Dontgib
  +FORCEYBILLBOARD
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    LZAB A 1 Bright A_JumpIf(scalex > 1.0, "Spawn2")
	TNT1 A 1 Bright A_SetScale(scalex+0.05, Scaley+1.0)
	Loop			
		Spawn2:
			LZAB A 0 A_Playsound("Gaster/Teleport", Chan_auto)
		Spawn3:
			LZAB A 1 Bright A_JumpIf(scalex < 0.1, "End")
			TNT1 A 1 Bright A_SetScale(scalex-0.05, scaley-0.0)
			Loop
		End:
			TNT1 A 0
			stop
	}
}

Actor Bossbox //Decorate by Fiendzy
{
	Radius 10
	Height 18
	scale 1.5
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		MANN A 1
	Corruptedspawn:
		MANN D 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SV_yourbestnightmare")
		MANN AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAABBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBCCCCCCCCCCCCCCCCCCCCCCCCCCCCDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDD 10
		goto RNGSpawn
	RNGSpawn:
		MANN D 1 A_Jump(256, "Bruisers", "CorruptFiend", "CorruptGosimer", "TrioSpawn", "Kartrape", "Dejavuspawn", "Zombiehordespawn", "ImpWarlordhordespawn", "Flemoidboss")
		goto Despawn
	Bruisers:
		MANN D 1 A_SpawnItemEx ("Bruiserdemon", 0, 48, 1, 0, 0, 0, 45, SXF_TELEFRAG|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION, 1)
		MANN D 1 A_spawnitemEX ("Bruiserdemon", 0, -48, 1, 0, 0, 0, 90, SXF_TELEFRAG|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION, 1)
		goto Despawn
	CorruptFiend:
		MANN D 1 A_SpawnItemEx ("Corrupt_Fiend", 0, 0, 1, 0, 0, 0, 0,SXF_TELEFRAG|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION, 1)
		goto Despawn
	CorruptGosimer:
		MANN D 1 A_SpawnItemEx ("Corrupt_Gosimer", 0, 48, 1, 0, 0, 0, 45, SXF_TELEFRAG|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION, 1)
		goto Despawn
	CorruptKunai:
		MANN D 1 A_SpawnItemEx ("Corrupt_Kunai", 0, -48, 1, 0, 0, 0, 90, SXF_TELEFRAG|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION, 1)
		goto Despawn
		
	Triospawn:
		MANN D 1 A_SpawnItemEx ("Corrupt_Fiend", 0, 0, 1, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_TELEFRAG|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION, 1)

//----------------------------------<Manncobox-Rewards!

 ACTOR Energy-Tank : UpgradeStamina //Fiends energy tank
 {
   Inventory.Amount 50
   Inventory.MaxAmount 200
   Inventory.pickupsound "ETANK"
   +Dontgib
   Inventory.PickupMessage "Soul Tank aquired! max health increased by 50!"
   states
   {
   Spawn:
      LIFE ABCDCB 4 BRIGHT
      loop
   Pickup:
      LIFE A 0 A_Playsound("ETANK",Chan_7)
      Stop
   }
 }

Actor Medbag : CustomInventory //
{
  Radius 4
  Height 18
  Inventory.RespawnTics "99999999"
  +INVENTORY.INVBAR
     +Dontgib
  Inventory.MaxAmount 3
  Inventory.InterHubAmount 3
  Inventory.Icon "I_MBPK"
  Inventory.PickupSound "MBackP"
  Inventory.PickupMessage "This item when dropped spits out Random Health!"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    MBPK A -1
    Stop
  Use:
    TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx ("Medicalbackpack", 0, 0, 28, 0, 0, 0, 0, 1)
    Stop
  }
}

    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR SimplyBackpack : CustomInventory
{
  +INVENTORY.AUTOACTIVATE
  +INVENTORY.ALWAYSPICKUP
  +INVENTORY.UNDROPPABLE
     +Dontgib
  Inventory.MaxAmount 0
  Height 26
  Inventory.PickupMessage "Picked up an ammo expansion!" // "Picked up a backpack full of ammo!"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    AMXP A 1
    loop
  Pickup:
	BPAK A 0 A_Jumpifinventory("Backpackcheck", 1, "Firstpickup")
    BPAK A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("Playerbackpackupgrade",0,0,0,0)
	BPAK A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("Peastolclip", 50)
	BPAK A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("Shellz", 4)
	BPAK A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("SuperShellz", 4)
	BPAK A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("AK_Mag", 75)
	BPAK A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("Roketammo", 5)
	BPAK A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("Battery", 40)
	BPAK A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("Railslugs", 5)
	BPAK A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("BFGCharge", 1)
	BPAK A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("Lightningammo", 25)
	Stop
  Firstpickup:
	BPAK a 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("FirstSimplyBackpack", 1)
    BPAK A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("Playerbackpackupgrade",0,0,0,0)
	BPAK A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("Peastolclip", 50)
	BPAK A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("Shellz", 4)
	BPAK A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("SuperShellz", 4)
	BPAK A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("AK_Mag", 75)
	BPAK A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("Roketammo", 5)
	BPAK A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("Battery", 40)
	BPAK A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("Railslugs", 5)
	BPAK A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("BFGCharge", 1)
	BPAK A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("Lightningammo", 25)
	BPAK A 0 A_TAKEINVENTORY("Backpackcheck", 1)
	Stop
  }
}

Actor Medicalbackpack
{
  Radius 1
  Height 1
     +Dontgib
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    MBPK A 15
    MBPK A 0 A_PlaySound("MBackP")
    MBPK A 5
  RNGSPAWN:
    MBPK A 0 A_Jump(253, 2)
    MBPK A 1 A_SpawnItemEx ("Hardberserk", 0, 0, 28, 0, 0, 0, 0, 1) 
   goto despawn
    MBPK A 0 A_Jump(255, 2)
    MBPK A 1 A_SpawnItemEx ("Medikit", 0, 0, 28, 0, 0, 0, 0, 1)  
   goto despawn
    MBPK A 0 A_Jump(255, 2)
    MBPK A 1 A_SpawnItemEx ("Stimpack", 0, 0, 28, 0, 0, 0, 0, 1) 
   goto despawn
    MBPK A 0
   Goto RNGSPAWN
  Despawn:
  MBPK A 1 A_FADEOUT(0.005)
  loop
  }
}

    TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx ("Spenserspawn37", 0, 0, 28, 0, 0, 0, 0, 1)
   goto despawn
      MBPK A 0 A_Jump(255, 2)
    TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx ("Spenserspawn38", 0, 0, 28, 0, 0, 0, 0, 1)
   goto despawn
      MBPK A 0 A_Jump(255, 2)
    TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx ("Spenserspawn39", 0, 0, 28, 0, 0, 0, 0, 1)
   goto despawn
      MBPK A 0 A_Jump(255, 2)
    TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx ("Spenserspawn40", 0, 0, 28, 0, 0, 0, 0, 1)
   goto despawn
    MBPK A 0 A_Jump(255, 2)
    TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx ("Spenserspawn41", 0, 0, 28, 0, 0, 0, 0, 1)
   goto despawn
    MBPK A 0
   Goto Randomdispenser
   Despawn:
    MBPK A 0
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR HardBerserkFiend : CustomInventory
{
  +COUNTITEM
     +Dontgib
  +INVENTORY.ALWAYSPICKUP
  Inventory.PickupMessage "$GOTBERSERK" // "Berserk!"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    PSTR A -1
    Stop
  Pickup:
    TNT1 A 0 A_Playsound("Jim/powerup",Chan_6)   
    TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("PowerStrength")
    TNT1 A 0 A_Giveinventory("Soulsphere4")
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR HardBerserk : CustomInventory
{
  +COUNTITEM
     +Dontgib
  +INVENTORY.ALWAYSPICKUP
  Inventory.PickupMessage "$GOTBERSERK" // "Berserk!"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    PSTR A -1
    Stop
  Pickup:
    TNT1 A 0 A_jumpifinventory("Fiendtoken",1,"Groovy")
    TNT1 A 0 A_Playsound("Duke/Vitamins",Chan_6)
    TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("PowerStrength")
    TNT1 A 0 HealThing(100, 0)
    Stop
  Groovy:
    TNT1 A 0 A_Giveinventory("HardBerserkFiend") 
  }
}


actor MegaMap : CustomInventory Replaces Allmap 
{
  +COUNTITEM
     +Dontgib
  +INVENTORY.FANCYPICKUPSOUND
  +INVENTORY.ALWAYSPICKUP
  Inventory.MaxAmount 0
  Inventory.PickupSound "misc/p_pkup"
  Inventory.PickupMessage "Mega Map!"
  states
  {
  Spawn:
    MMAP ABCDCB 6 Bright
    Loop
  Pickup:
    TNT1 A 1 A_GiveInventory ("Allmap")
    TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory ("DoomScanner")
    stop
  }
}

actor DoomScanner : PowerupGiver
{
  powerup.type "Scanner"
  +INVENTORY.AUTOACTIVATE
  states
  {
  Spawn:
    TNT1 A 1
    stop
  }
}

Actor bagspawnerGosimersAmmoSphere : Custominventory
{
	Game Doom
	+INVENTORY.AUTOACTIVATE
	+INVENTORY.ALWAYSPICKUP
	+INVENTORY.FANCYPICKUPSOUND
	Inventory.PickupMessage "Infinite Ammo!"
	Inventory.PickupSound "misc/p_pkup"
	States
	{
  Spawn:
    SOUL A 4 BRIGHT
    Loop
  pickup:   
    TNT1 A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("Gosimersbackpack")
    TNT1 A 0 A_GIVEINVENTORY("GosimersAmmoSphere")
    Stop
    }
}

Actor Joy : Custominventory
{
	Game Doom
	scale 0.05
	   +Dontgib
	Inventory.PickupMessage "Joy... Do you have it in you?"
  	Inventory.RespawnTics "99999999"
	+INVENTORY.INVBAR
	Inventory.MaxAmount 1
 	Inventory.InterHubAmount 1
 	Inventory.Icon "I_FJOY"
	Inventory.PickupSound "Joy/Pickup"
	States
	{
  Spawn:
    FJOY A 4 BRIGHT
    Loop
   use:   
    TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("UsedJoy",0,0,0,0)
    TNT1 A 0 A_Giveinventory("Soulsphere4")
    TNT1 A 0 A_Giveinventory("Soulsphere4")
    TNT1 A 0 A_Giveinventory("Joyspeed")
    TNT1 A 0 A_Giveinventory("joyDoubleDamage")
    TNT1 A 0 A_Giveinventory("Joyresistance")
    TNT1 A 0 A_Takeinventory("Joy")
    }
}
